[30;1m488 | [0m[35m   problem. However, in degenerate cases, this expansion might have _no effect_[0m
[30;1m489 | [0m[35m   on the collision count, causing a failure mode where a linear sequence of[0m
[30;1m490 | [0m[35m   insertion leads to exponential storage growth.[0m

[30;1m141 | [0m[35m  smart/unique pointers and callbacks could lead to undefined behavior. A later[0m

[30;1m181 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m182 | [0m[35m2. Building all extensions with Bazel through a subprocess, by extending[0m
[30;1m183 | [0m[35ma Python build backend such as ``setuptools``. This allows you to stick to[0m
[30;1m184 | [0m[35mthose well-established build tools, like ``setuptools``, at the expense[0m
[30;1m185 | [0m[35mof more boilerplate Python code and slower build times, since Bazel is[0m
